name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r

rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 25, 2024
msg:Newly opened in 2023, the shareholder is still Changchun Sino-Japanese Club. In terms of hardware, it is now the best in Changchun. The decoration and facilities are all new. There are chairs in the elevator, which are quite user-friendly. There is a refrigerator and free mini-bar drinks in the room, a smart toilet, and a large bathtub, not the small one in Shangri-La. Bath salts are provided, which makes it very comfortable to soak. Outside the window is the Yitong River. Originally, the view of the rooms facing west in Hyatt was the best in Changchun, but now that an unfinished building has been built to the west of Hyatt, the view outside the window is completely ruined. I am not in the mood to look at it. The view outside the window of Yinlu can now be said to be the best in Changchun.

The dining is pretty good. There are singers in the barbecue restaurant downstairs at night. The Japanese restaurant has very distinctive cuisine and is the best Japanese food in Changchun.

The gym is next to the swimming pool, the equipment is brand new, and there are lifeguards in the swimming pool. The only drawback is that the gym can be equipped with a water dispenser and paper towels.

What needs to be improved is that the yukata in the room is a short Japanese yukata, which is a bit embarrassing for tall men. It is recommended to provide two options of long and short. In addition, the rooms facing the Yitong River face west. In Changchun, the main wind blows in winter, and the rooms have floor-to-ceiling windows so it will be a bit cold. However, the view from the west-facing rooms should be very good in summer.
